 1) cricket ke itihaas main pehali baar de-nite test australia ke edilade main khelaa gaya
 The match saw 47,441 viewers on the first day, 42,372 on the second day, 33,923 on the third day
 yani kul milkaar 1,23,736 darshakon ne teenon din match dekha
 2) Although cricket was born in England, Australia has won the first match of all cricket formats
 australia ne 1877 main khele gaye pehle test match main england ko 45 ran se haraaya tha
 The first ODI was played between Australia and England in 1971
 ise bhi kangaroo team ne 5 ran se jeeta
 The first day-night ODI also went to Australia
 is match main australia ne west indies ko 5 wicket se haraaya tha
 If we talk about the T20 match, this is also the first time Australia has won
 kangaroo team ne 44 ran se newzealand ko is match main haraaya tha
 Now Australia also emerged victorious in the first day-night test
 yahaan kiwi team ko 3 wicket se kangarooon ne haraaya
 3) The first day-night ODI match was played on 27 November 1979 in Sydney, Australia
 is saal pehle de-nite test match bhi 27 november ko shuru hua
 4) Australia won the Test by 3 wickets in Adelaide and won the series 2–0
 is jeet ke saath hi australia isisi test ranking main number do par pahunch gai
 5) New Zealand team has lost a Test series for the first time since 2013
 is dauraan kiwi team ne chaar series jiti or teen series drow khelin
 The last time England defeated the Kiwi team was in a 2–0 Test series in 2013
 6) australia or newzealand ke bich hue edilade de-nite test main ek bhi ballebaaz shatak nahin laga paaya
 Earlier in 1993, there were no centuries in the Test matches of West Indies and Australia at the same ground
 match main sarvaadhik score richi richardsan ke naam rahaa, unhone 72 ran banaae the
 7) In this Test, the score of 66 runs was scored by wicketkeeper Peter Navy
 ye edilade maidan par kisi bhi ballebaaz kaa sabase kam score he
 Earlier in 1951, Australia's Doug Ring scored 67 against the West Indies
 8) australia ke josh hezalwood ne test kii teesri pari main 70 ran dekar 6 wicket liye or test main 136 ran dekar kul 9 wicket liye
 Hazelwood's best performance in this test
 tippaniyan 9) For the first time in the last 64 years in Adelaide, a test has ended in three days
 isse pehle 1951 main west indies ne australia ko isi maidan par teen din main 6 wicket se haraaya tha
 In that match, Australia won the toss and bat first and lost the match
 is baar newzealand ne toss jitkar ballebaazi chuni or match haar gai
 10) Nagpur Test played between India and South Africa also ended in three days
 is match main kul 247
 652 runs in 5 overs and 40 wickets fall
 edilade de-nite test bhi teen din main khatm hua
 251 in this match
 2 over main 821 ran bane or kul 37 wicket gire
